<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #999999; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Independent_politician" title="Independent politician">Independent</a></div>
<div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #ff4c7f; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Scottish_Senior_Citizens_Unity_Party" title="Scottish Senior Citizens Unity Party">SSCUP</a></div>
</td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #C10000; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Scottish_Socialist_Party" title="Scottish Socialist Party">Socialist</a></div>
<div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #00C000; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Scottish_Green_Party" title="Scottish Green Party">Greens</a></div>
</td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:dodgerblue; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Scottish_Conservative_Party" class="mw-redirect" title="Scottish Conservative Party">Conservative</a></div>
<div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FFFF00; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Scottish_National_Party" title="Scottish National Party">SNP</a></div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>There have been five elections to the Parliament, in <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_election,_1999" title="Scottish Parliament election, 1999">1999</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_election,_2003" title="Scottish Parliament election, 2003">2003</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_election,_2007" title="Scottish Parliament election, 2007">2007</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_general_election,_2011" class="mw-redirect" title="Scottish Parliament general election, 2011">2011</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_election,_2016" title="Scottish Parliament election, 2016">2016</a>.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Next_Scottish_Parliament_election" title="Next Scottish Parliament election">next Scottish Parliament election</a> is due to be held on Thursday 6 May 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-dates_act_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dates_act-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> Under the <a href="/wiki/Scotland_Act_1998" title="Scotland Act 1998">Scotland Act 1998</a>, an ordinary general election to the Scottish Parliament would normally have been held on the first Thursday in May four years after the <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_election,_2016" title="Scottish Parliament election, 2016">2016 election</a>, i.e. in May 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-ScotlandAct1_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ScotlandAct1-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> This would have clashed with the proposed date of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_general_election,_2017" title="United Kingdom general election, 2017">2020 United Kingdom general election</a>, but later became a moot point after the latter was brought forward to 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-clash_81-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-clash-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> In November 2015, the Scottish Government published a Scottish Elections (Dates) Bill, which proposed to extend the term of the Parliament to five years.<sup id="cite_ref-clash_81-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-clash-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> That Bill was passed by the Scottish Parliament on 25 February 2016 and received Royal Assent on 30 March 2016, setting the new date for the election as 6 May 2021, with subsequent elections every four years after that.<sup id="cite_ref-dates_act_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dates_act-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As with all elections in the UK, Irish and qualifying <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth</a> citizens are entitled to vote.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Unlike elections to <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Parliament of the United Kingdom">the Westminster parliament</a>, citizens of other non-Commonwealth <a href="/wiki/Member_state_of_the_European_Union" title="Member state of the European Union">EU member states</a> who are resident in Scotland are entitled to vote in elections to the Scottish Parliament. Overseas electors on Scottish <a href="/wiki/Electoral_register" class="mw-redirect" title="Electoral register">electoral registers</a> are not allowed to vote in Scottish Parliament elections. From the <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_election,_2016" title="Scottish Parliament election, 2016">2016</a> election, the franchise for Scottish Parliament elections was expanded to include 16 and 17-year olds.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Current_composition">Current composition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Scottish_Parliament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Current composition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Criticism">Criticism</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Scottish_Parliament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Criticism">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For criticisms of the Scottish Parliament Building, see <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Parliament_Building#Controversy" title="Scottish Parliament Building">Scottish Parliament Building §&#160;Controversy</a>.</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg/170px-Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg/255px-Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg/340px-Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg 2x" data-file-width="766" data-file-height="1024" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Wfm_scottish_parliament_construction.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Enric Miralles' Scottish Parliament complex in Holyrood Park during construction. The building was completed in 2004. Above and behind the new Parliament is the neoclassical <a href="/wiki/Old_Royal_High_School" title="Old Royal High School">Old Royal High School</a>, which was prepared for a previous devolved Scottish parliament, but never used.</div></div></div>
<p>The resignation of <a href="/wiki/Henry_McLeish" title="Henry McLeish">Henry McLeish</a> as First Minister, brought on by an <a href="/wiki/Officegate" title="Officegate">office expenses scandal</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> generated controversy in the first years of the Parliament.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Various academics have written on how the Scottish Parliament can be improved as a governing institution.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="West_Lothian_question">West Lothian question</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Scottish_Parliament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: West Lothian question">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/West_Lothian_question" title="West Lothian question">West Lothian question</a></div>
<p>A procedural consequence of the establishment of the Scottish Parliament is that Scottish MPs sitting in the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="House of Commons of the United Kingdom">UK House of Commons</a> have been able to vote on domestic legislation that applies only to England, Wales and Northern Ireland – whilst English, Scottish, Welsh and Northern Irish Westminster MPs are unable to vote on the domestic legislation of the Scottish Parliament. This phenomenon is known as the West Lothian question and has led to criticism.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> Following the Conservative victory in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_general_election,_2015" title="United Kingdom general election, 2015">2015 UK election</a>, <a href="/wiki/Parliamentary_procedure" title="Parliamentary procedure">standing orders</a> of the House of Commons were changed to give MPs representing English constituencies a new "veto" over laws only affecting England, known as <a href="/wiki/English_votes_for_English_laws" title="English votes for English laws">English votes for English laws</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Parliamentary_Association" title="Commonwealth Parliamentary Association">Commonwealth Parliamentary Association</a></li></ul>
</div></td></tr><tr><td class="navbox-abovebelow" colspan="2"><div><sup><small>1</small></sup> <a href="/wiki/European_Union_law" title="European Union law">European Union law</a> applies in the United Kingdom and <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">Gibraltar</a>. Following the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_invocation_of_Article_50_of_the_Treaty_on_European_Union" title="United Kingdom invocation of Article 50 of the Treaty on European Union">invokation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Withdrawal_from_the_European_Union" title="Withdrawal from the European Union">Article 50</a>, the United Kingdom is <a href="/wiki/Brexit" title="Brexit">set to leave</a> the European Union. A <a href="/wiki/European_Union_(Withdrawal)_Act_2018" title="European Union (Withdrawal) Act 2018">Great Repeal Bill</a> has been proposed to incorporate all <i>current</i> European laws into <a href="/wiki/Law_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Law of the United Kingdom">British law</a>.
<br /><sup><small>2</small></sup> "Bailiwick-wide" legislature passed in the <a href="/wiki/States_of_Guernsey" title="States of Guernsey">States of Guernsey</a> applies not only in <a href="/wiki/Guernsey" title="Guernsey">Guernsey</a>, but also in <a href="/wiki/Alderney" title="Alderney">Alderney</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sark" title="Sark">Sark</a>, with the consent of their governments.</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
